# CAMEO VERB PATTERN DICTIONARY
# SYNSET TRANSLATION INTO SPANISH

# Javier Osorio, John Jay College of Criminal Justice
# Last Update: 2/13/2017
#
# The source for these Synonym sets (Synsets) is file CAMEO 2.0
# These Synsets use the original name of the Synset in English,
# but the content is in Spanish. In this way, the translation does
# not affect the structure of the Cameo rule.
#
